#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Regulate the Monasteries

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_While the spiritual richness of the leading monasteries of our country is a constant asset for our ruler these monasteries also have a tendency to lapse into corruption and lacking discipline. We must curb the excesses of the monks and create set of strict laws with harsh punishments for those who falter, be they individual monks or entire orders._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Vajrayana.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Vajrayana.png/28px-Vajrayana.png)](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") Vajrayana.
*   has an [![Administrative technology.png](/images/8/8e/Administrative_technology.png)](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology") [administrative technology](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology") of at least level 15.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Regulated Monastic Law’_.

Allow

[Ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Regulated Monastic Law’_ for the rest of the campaign with the following effects:

*   [![Tolerance of the true faith.png](/images/thumb/d/d9/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png/28px-Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png)](/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith "Tolerance of the true faith") **+1** tolerance of the true faith,
*   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier") **+5%** stability cost modifier.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Invite a Lama to Settle in Our Country

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_We should invite a powerful Lama to settle in our capital. By patronizing this man and his future reincarnations we may create a lasting legacy for our dynasty._

* * *

[![Common Sense.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Common_Sense.png/28px-Common_Sense.png)](/Common_Sense "Common Sense")

Available only with the [Common Sense](/Common_Sense "Common Sense") DLC enabled.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Vajrayana.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Vajrayana.png/28px-Vajrayana.png)](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") Vajrayana.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Lama’_.
*   did _not_ have this event during the reign of the current [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler").

Allow

The country:

*   is _not_ at [war](/War "War").
*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** stability.
*   has at least [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige") **25** prestige.

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   loses [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige") **25** prestige.
*   gets the [![Msg event.png](/images/thumb/4/4e/Msg_event.png/20px-Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event") event ‘[Messenger Returns from Tibet](/Buddhism_events#buddhism_events.34 "Buddhism events")’ in 60 days.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Anti-Christian Edict

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Prevent any possible undermining of authority that Christianity may cause by issuing an edict to expel all Christian missionaries and demand that all converts renounce their new faith._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   has a religion of the [Eastern denominations](/Eastern_denominations "Eastern denominations").
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Anti-Christian Edict’_.
*   has a [Christian](/Christian "Christian") neighbor _or_ a Christian country owns Sakam (738), Kingchow (666) _or_ Macau (668).

Allow

The country:

*   is _not_ the [Defender of the Faith](/Defender_of_the_Faith "Defender of the Faith").

A Christian neighbor of the country _or_ the Christian country that owns Sakam (738), Kingchow (666) _or_ Macau (668) has an [![Opinion.png](/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion") opinion of less than **0** towards the country.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Anti-Christian Edict’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+2%** missionary strength,
*   [![Improve relations.png](/images/thumb/4/46/Improve_relations.png/28px-Improve_relations.png)](/Improve_relations "Improve relations") **−10%** improve relations.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Enforce our Heritage

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Our faith is the honored way of our ancestors. We cannot allow foreign faiths to encroach on our traditions._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   has a religion of the [Eastern denominations](/Eastern_denominations "Eastern denominations").
*   does **not** have the modifier _‘Enforcing our Heritage’_.

If the [![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven") ‘Mandate of Heaven’ DLC is enabled then the country can _not_ be [![Confucianism](/images/thumb/a/a2/Confucianism.png/28px-Confucianism.png)](/Confucian "Confucian") [Confucian](/Confucian "Confucian").

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** [stability](/Stability "Stability").
*   borders a country that does _not_ follow a religion of the [Eastern denominations](/Eastern_denominations "Eastern denominations").

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Enforcing our Heritage’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+2%** missionary strength,
*   [![Tolerance heathen.png](/images/thumb/d/dc/Tolerance_heathen.png/28px-Tolerance_heathen.png)](/Tolerance_of_heathens "Tolerance of heathens") **−1** tolerance of heathens.

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Renovate the Emerald Buddha Shrine (§YKarma +§!)

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

* * *

_The shrine holding the sacred Emerald Buddha is in need of renovation, not only for the sake of its material maintenance but also so that it emphasizes the aspects of Buddhism that are presently useful to the state._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Theravada.png](/images/thumb/5/52/Theravada.png/28px-Theravada.png)](/Theravada "Theravada") Theravada, [![Mahayana.png](/images/thumb/2/2f/Mahayana.png/28px-Mahayana.png)](/Mahayana "Mahayana") Mahayana _or_ [![Vajrayana.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Vajrayana.png/28px-Vajrayana.png)](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") Vajrayana
*   owns any province with modifier _“The Emerald Buddha”_

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Gold Icon.png](/images/2/26/Gold_Icon.png)](/Ducats "Ducats") **0.25** years' worth of income

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   loses [![Gold Icon.png](/images/2/26/Gold_Icon.png)](/Ducats "Ducats") ducats equal to **0.25** years of income
*   If any owned province has modifier _“The Emerald Buddha”_
    *   Remove modifier _"The Emerald Buddha"_
    *   [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital gains permanent province modifier _“The Emerald Buddha”_ for the rest of the game, giving the following effects:
        *   [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Yearly_prestige "Yearly prestige") **+0.5** Yearly prestige
        *   [![Monthly karma](/images/thumb/2/24/Monthly_karma.png/28px-Monthly_karma.png)](/Karma "Monthly karma") **−0.1** Monthly karma

### Shinto\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=18 "Edit section: Shinto") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=18 "Edit section: Shinto")\]

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Baptize Ruler

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_The Christian community in our lands is growing ever stronger and some feel that the time has come to welcome this western God on a personal level. If our ruler converts to Christianity some might find it an affront to traditions, but it may also come with considerable benefits._

* * *

[![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven")

Available only with the [Mandate of Heaven](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven") DLC enabled.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Shintoism](/images/thumb/8/85/Shinto.png/28px-Shinto.png)](/Shinto "Shinto") Shinto.
*   has the [incident](/Isolationism "Isolationism") ‘Spread of Christianity’ _or_ has an heir with Christian tutors[\[1\]](#cite_note-1).
*   does **not** have the modifier _‘Christian Ruler’_.

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **2** [stability](/Stability "Stability").
*   does **not** have a [regency](/Regency "Regency").

* * *

Effects

The ruler and the heir of the country:

*   become [![Catholicism](/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic") Catholic.

The ruler gets the modifier _‘Christian Ruler’_ until the ruler changes with the following effects:

*   [![Tolerance of the true faith.png](/images/thumb/d/d9/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png/28px-Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png)](/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith "Tolerance of the true faith") **−1** tolerance of the true faith,
*   [![Institution spread.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Institution_spread.png/28px-Institution_spread.png)](/Institution_spread "Institution spread") **+5%** institution spread,
*   [![Trade efficiency.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Trade_efficiency.png/28px-Trade_efficiency.png)](/Trade_efficiency "Trade efficiency") **+10%** trade efficiency.

If the country has the incident ‘Spread of Christianity’

*   the move **+1** toward open end of the incident.

### Dharmic\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=19 "Edit section: Dharmic") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=19 "Edit section: Dharmic")\]

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Introduce Din-i Illahi

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Reduce social unrest caused by religious disagreements between our subjects by introducing a new religious doctrine that will attempt to merge the principal thoughts of Islam with Hinduism._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The [![Dharma.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Dharma.png/28px-Dharma.png)](/Dharma "Dharma")‘Dharma’ DLC is _not_ enabled.

The country:

*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Divine Faith’_.
*   is either [![Hinduism](/images/thumb/1/1a/Hinduism.png/28px-Hinduism.png)](/Hindu "Hindu") Hindu and owns a Muslim province _or_ is Muslim [![Flag of Mughals](/images/thumb/e/e6/Mughals.png/20px-Mughals.png)](/Mughals "Mughals") [Mughals](/Mughals "Mughals") and owns a Hindu province.

Allow

The country:

*   is _not_ the [![Become Defender of the Faith.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/Become_Defender_of_the_Faith.png/28px-Become_Defender_of_the_Faith.png)](/Defender_of_the_faith "Defender of the faith") [Defender of the Faith](/Defender_of_the_Faith "Defender of the Faith").
*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Divine Faith’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effect:

*   [![Technology cost.png](/images/thumb/e/ea/Technology_cost.png/28px-Technology_cost.png)](/Technology_cost "Technology cost") **−6%** technology cost.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Anti-Muslim edict

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

*   does _not_ own a [![Sunni Islam](/images/thumb/2/2f/Sunni.png/28px-Sunni.png)](/Sunni "Sunni") [Sunni](/Sunni "Sunni") province.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Anti-Muslim edict’_.

*   [![Tolerance heathen.png](/images/thumb/d/dc/Tolerance_heathen.png/28px-Tolerance_heathen.png)](/Tolerance_of_heathens "Tolerance of heathens") **−2** tolerance of heathens,
*   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+0.5%** missionary strength.

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Accept Religious Sects

*   is _not_ at [war](/War "War").

*   [![Missionary strength vs heretics.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/Missionary_strength_vs_heretics.png/28px-Missionary_strength_vs_heretics.png)](/Missionary_strength_vs_heretics "Missionary strength vs heretics") **−2%** missionary strength vs heretics.

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Support the Haridasa Movement

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

* * *

_Support the spiritual Haridasa movement in its efforts to promote Madhvacharya's philosophical school of dualism as opposed to Adi Shankara's non-dualistic ideals._

* * *

*   is [![Hinduism](/images/thumb/1/1a/Hinduism.png/28px-Hinduism.png)](/Hindu "Hindu") Hindu.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Haridasa Movement Support’_.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Advaita Movement Support’_.

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** stability.
*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Diplomatic power.png](/images/d/da/Diplomatic_power.png)](/Diplomatic_power "Diplomatic power") diplomatic skill is at least 3.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Haridasa Movement Support’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+2%** missionary strength,
*   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier") **−10%** stability cost modifier.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Support the Advaita Movement

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Support the spiritual Advaita movement in its efforts to promote the non-dualistic ideals of Adi Shankara as opposed to Madhvacharya's philosophical school of dualism._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Hinduism](/images/thumb/1/1a/Hinduism.png/28px-Hinduism.png)](/Hindu "Hindu") Hindu.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Advaita Movement Support’_.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Haridasa Movement Support’_.

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** stability.
*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Advaita Movement Support’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+2%** missionary strength,
*   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") **−1** national unrest.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Save the Burning World

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Our faith was born seeking unity where there was discord and the belief that God was above the religious divides of the world. However, if we are to put out the fires of sin in this world, we need people to embrace the truth._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Sikhism](/images/thumb/f/f0/Sikh.png/28px-Sikh.png)](/Sikh "Sikh") Sikh.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Saving the Burning World’_.

Allow

[Ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Saving the Burning World’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+3%** missionary strength,
*   [![Tolerance heretic.png](/images/thumb/2/27/Tolerance_heretic.png/28px-Tolerance_heretic.png)](/Tolerance_of_heretics "Tolerance of heretics") **−1** tolerance of heretics.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Choose Personal Deity Again

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.33.

* * *

_Sometimes, one regrets one's choices. Why should one's choice as a young man of which deity to follow apply for the rest of one's life? Fortunately, our arrangements with the Brahmins allow us some flexibility on the matter._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Hinduism](/images/thumb/1/1a/Hinduism.png/28px-Hinduism.png)](/Hindu "Hindu") Hindu
*   has [![Brahmins.png](/images/thumb/f/f2/Brahmins.png/28px-Brahmins.png)](/Brahmins "Brahmins") Brahmins estate

Allow

The country:

*   Is _not_ in a regency
*   Has the _“Choice of Personal Deities”_ estate privilege
*   Does have a personal deity
*   Did _not_ enact this [![Decision.png](/images/thumb/b/b1/Decision.png/20px-Decision.png)](/Decision "Decision") decision in the last 20 years

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   Loses [![Legitimacy.png](/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy") **25** legitimacy (or equivalent)
*   Loses [![Republican tradition.png](/images/e/ee/Republican_tradition.png)](/Republic_tradition "Republic tradition") **12** republican tradition
*   Trigger country event _“[Paths of Hinduism](/Hinduism_events#hindu_events.1 "Hinduism events")”_

### Pagan\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=20 "Edit section: Pagan") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=20 "Edit section: Pagan")\]

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Adopt Vajrayana Buddhism

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_The religion of Tibet is a powerful tool and Buddhism was once championed by great empires. Let us convert our country to this powerful new religion and learn the value of peace and discipline._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [Pagan](/Pagan "Pagan").
*   is _not_ a [subject nation](/Subject_nation "Subject nation") other than a [tributary state](/Tributary_state "Tributary state").
*   either has [![Vajrayana.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Vajrayana.png/28px-Vajrayana.png)](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") Vajrayana as [dominant religion](/Dominant_religion "Dominant religion"), or owns a province that is [![Vajrayana.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Vajrayana.png/28px-Vajrayana.png)](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") Vajrayana and it is at least the [![Age of Absolutism.png](/images/thumb/e/ec/Age_of_Absolutism.png/28px-Age_of_Absolutism.png)](/Age_of_Absolutism "Age of Absolutism") age of absolutism.

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** stability.
*   is _not_ at [war](/War "War").

If the country has a [secondary religion](/Secondary_religion "Secondary religion") then it must be [![Vajrayana.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Vajrayana.png/28px-Vajrayana.png)](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") Vajrayana.

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   becomes [![Vajrayana.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Vajrayana.png/28px-Vajrayana.png)](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") Vajrayana.
*   loses [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **4** stability.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Encourage Divination

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Make divination a fundamental basis of our society, whether it is used to drive away ill spirits or ascertain information from the gods regarding sacrifices and illnesses._

*   is [Pagan](/Pagan "Pagan").
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Divination’_.

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** stability.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Divination’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") **−1** national unrest,
*   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier") **+5%** stability cost modifier.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Religious Sacrifices

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

_Turn religious sacrifices of animals and bloodletting into a common practice in our society to please the gods._

*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Religious Sacrifices’_.

Allow

The country:

*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.
*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** stability.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Religious Sacrifices’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Yearly_prestige "Yearly prestige") **+1** yearly prestige,
*   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier") **−20%** stability cost modifier.

### Animist\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=21 "Edit section: Animist") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=21 "Edit section: Animist")\]

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Ritual Education

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_The belief that there is just one divine being in the world is a horrible myth that seems widespread wherever we go. We must endeavor to educate our poor subjects in the true nature of things, of how the world functions and of the many spirits that inhabit it._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Animism](/images/thumb/1/18/Animist.png/28px-Animist.png)](/Animist "Animist") Animist.
*   owns a province that is _not_ Animist.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Ritual Education’_.

Allow

The country:

*   has an [![Administrative technology.png](/images/8/8e/Administrative_technology.png)](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology") [administrative technology](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology") of at least level 8.
*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **2** stability.
*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.
*   has at least [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") 50 administrative power.

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   loses [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **50** administrative power.
*   gets the modifier _‘Ritual Education’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effect:
    *   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+2%** missionary strength.

### Fetishist\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=22 "Edit section: Fetishist") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=22 "Edit section: Fetishist")\]

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Wandering Shamans

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_We have come to control areas far beyond the limits of our faith and as a result a great number of heathens look to us for guidance. Let us send forth our Shamans to spread our faith and to teach those among our new subjects who are able to become Shamans themselves._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Fetishist](/images/thumb/8/8d/Fetishist.png/28px-Fetishist.png)](/Fetishist "Fetishist") Fetishist.
*   owns a province that is _not_ Fetishist.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Wandering Shamans’_.

Allow

The country:

*   has an [![Administrative technology.png](/images/8/8e/Administrative_technology.png)](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology") [administrative technology](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology") of at least level 8.
*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **2** stability.
*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.
*   has at least [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") 50 administrative power.

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   loses [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **50** administrative power.
*   gets the modifier _‘Wandering Shamans’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effect:
    *   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength")**+2%** missionary strength.

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Send the Shaman to foreign Cults

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.33.

* * *

_We can send the shaman of our \[Root.GovernmentName\] to a country with a foreign cult in order to study the religious and cult practices of said country._

* * *

[![Rights of Man.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Rights_of_Man.png/28px-Rights_of_Man.png)](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man")

Available only with the [Rights of Man](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man") DLC enabled.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   Is [![Fetishist](/images/thumb/8/8d/Fetishist.png/28px-Fetishist.png)](/Fetishist "Fetishist") Fetishist
*   Has selected the option _"Wait, you are still needed here, shaman!"_ during [![Msg event.png](/images/4/4e/Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event") _"[The Quest for a new Cult](/Fetishist_events#fetishist_flavor.601 "Fetishist events")"_ event

Allow

Uses [cult mechanism](/Pagan_denominations#Cults "Pagan denominations")

* * *

Effects

Trigger [![Msg event.png](/images/4/4e/Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event") _"[The Quest for a new Cult](/Fetishist_events#fetishist_flavor.601 "Fetishist events")"_ event

* * *

AI will **never** take this decision.

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Switch Primary Cult

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.33.

* * *

_The \[Root.Monarch.GetTitle\] of our \[Root.GovernmentName\] has the authority to select a new Primary Cult for \[Root.GetName\]. Choosing so will however upset our people._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

[![Clergy.png](/images/thumb/0/0e/Clergy.png/28px-Clergy.png)](/Clergy "Clergy") Clergy privilege [![Privilege singular cult.png](/images/thumb/a/ab/Privilege_singular_cult.png/28px-Privilege_singular_cult.png)](/File:Privilege_singular_cult.png) _"Embrace Singular Cult"_ is active

Allow

*   Does _not_ have country modifier _“Change of Traditions”_
*   Has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **0** Stability

* * *

Effects

*   Lose [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** stability
*   Gain _“Change of Traditions”_ for [![Time Icon.png](/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time") **50** years, giving:
    *   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost "Stability cost") **+10%** Stability cost modifier
    *   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") **+1** National unrest
*   Trigger [![Msg event.png](/images/4/4e/Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event") _“[The Primary Cult of \[Root.GetName\]](/Fetishist_events#fetishist_flavor.602 "Fetishist events")”_ event

* * *

AI will **never** take this decision.

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Choose a new Cult

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.33.

* * *

_The faith of \[Root.Religion.GetName\] is not a rigid one with only one deity. We believe in a collection of different deities and cults, who worship said deities. From time to time it is necessary for a ruler to change the focus of worship for the country though. With the help of our \[Root.GetClergyName\] we can swap the focus quite easily._

* * *

[![Rights of Man.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Rights_of_Man.png/28px-Rights_of_Man.png)](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man")

Available only with the [Rights of Man](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man") DLC enabled.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   Is [![Fetishist](/images/thumb/8/8d/Fetishist.png/28px-Fetishist.png)](/Fetishist "Fetishist") Fetishist
*   At least one of:
    *   Has completed the [![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions") [![Flag of Oyo](/images/thumb/5/5b/Oyo.png/20px-Oyo.png)](/Oyo "Oyo") [Oyo](/Oyo "Oyo")'s mission _"[Gather Cults](/Oyo_missions#Gather_Cults "Oyo missions")"_
    *   [![Clergy.png](/images/thumb/0/0e/Clergy.png/28px-Clergy.png)](/Clergy "Clergy") Clergy privilege [![Privilege switch hindu deity.png](/images/thumb/c/c1/Privilege_switch_hindu_deity.png/28px-Privilege_switch_hindu_deity.png)](/File:Privilege_switch_hindu_deity.png) _"Flexible Cult"_ is active

Allow

The country:

*   Is _not_ in a regency
*   Has adopted any cult
*   If is a [![Government republic.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Government_republic.png/28px-Government_republic.png)](/Republic "Republic") republic
    *   Has at least [![Republican tradition.png](/images/e/ee/Republican_tradition.png)](/Republic_tradition "Republic tradition") **12** Republican tradition
*   Else:
    *   Has at least [![Legitimacy.png](/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy") **25** Legitimacy (or equivalent)

Can take this decision once every [![Time Icon.png](/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time") **20** years

* * *

Effects

*   If is a [![Government republic.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Government_republic.png/28px-Government_republic.png)](/Republic "Republic") republic
    *   Has at least [![Republican tradition.png](/images/e/ee/Republican_tradition.png)](/Republic_tradition "Republic tradition") **5** Republican tradition
*   Else:
    *   Has at least [![Legitimacy.png](/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy") **10** Legitimacy (or equivalent)
*   Trigger [![Msg event.png](/images/4/4e/Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event") _“[A new Cult for \[Root.GetName\]](/Fetishist_events#fetishist_flavor.603 "Fetishist events")”_ event

* * *

AI will **never** take this decision.

_It is high time we take a stand for the faith of our ancestors. Let us do away with all syncretism and outside traditions and promote a purer version of our religion._

*   owns a province that is _not_ Totemist.

*   has at least [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") 50 administrative power.

* * *

Effects

    *   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength")**+2%** missionary strength.

### Norse\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=24 "Edit section: Norse") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=24 "Edit section: Norse")\]

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Spreading of Norse Rituals

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Converting to the Norse religion requires nothing, every person is able to direct their own religious rituals. As long as you honor the Aesirs - Odin, Thor, Freja and Snotra - you are considered a follower of the Asatru. Let us encourage more and more of our subjects to learn of our gods so that they can at least start to worship them_

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Norse.png](/images/thumb/c/ce/Norse.png/28px-Norse.png)](/Norse "Norse") Norse.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Spreading of Rituals’_.

Allow

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Spreading of Rituals’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effect:

*   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+1%** missionary strength.

### Tengri\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=25 "Edit section: Tengri") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=25 "Edit section: Tengri")\]

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Yellow Shamanism

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Since the days of the Great Khans many of our subjects are followers of Vajrayana Buddhism and while we lament that they have strayed from the pure faith of our nation it would be unwise to turn them away. Let us instead accentuate the syncretic elements of our faith and borrow from the Vajrayana rituals and include these Buddhists in our community._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Tengri](/images/thumb/9/9f/Tengri.png/28px-Tengri.png)](/Tengri "Tengri") Tengri.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Yellow Shamanism’_.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Black Shamanism’_.

Allow

[Ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Yellow Shamanism’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effect:

*   [![Tolerance heathen.png](/images/thumb/d/dc/Tolerance_heathen.png/28px-Tolerance_heathen.png)](/Tolerance_of_heathens "Tolerance of heathens") **+2** tolerance of heathens.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Black Shamanism

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Buddhism is spreading among the practitioners of our ancestral faith at an alarming rate. While this faith was accepted by some of our ancestors it is now dangerously pushing back the true Tengriist faith and polluting the practices of our subjects with Buddhist tendencies. We must actively reject such notions and instead work to spread the true and pure practices of our ancestors among our people._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Tengri](/images/thumb/9/9f/Tengri.png/28px-Tengri.png)](/Tengri "Tengri") Tengri.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Black Shamanism’_.
*   does _not_ have a [secondary religion](/Secondary_religion "Secondary religion").

Allow

The country:

*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Yellow Shamanism’_.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Black Shamanism’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effect:

*   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+2%** missionary strength.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Expel the Khojas

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Over time the influence of the Khoja and his descendants has grown dangerously strong in our country. Now that they do not have the ear of our ruler we can forcibly expel them from our lands, avoiding future conflicts._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Tengri](/images/thumb/9/9f/Tengri.png/28px-Tengri.png)](/Tengri "Tengri") Tengri.
*   owns at least 2 [cities](/Cities "Cities").
*   had the event ‘[Popular Sufi Teacher](/Tengri_events#tengri_events.16 "Tengri events")’ and chosen the option “Let him serve the throne!” and afther this the country did _not_ change its secondary religion.
*   has _not_ enacted this decision _nor_ chosen the option “No, he is too dangerous” of the event ‘Popular Sufi Teacher’ _nor_ the event ‘[The Khoja takes power](/Tengri_events#tengri_events.18 "Tengri events")’.

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Legitimacy.png](/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy") 75 [legitimacy](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy") _or_ equivalent.
*   does _not_ have the ruler modifier _‘Support of the Khoja’_.

* * *

Effects

_The Khoja and his descendants will not bother us again._  
[![Sunni rebels.png](/images/thumb/6/66/Sunni_rebels.png/20px-Sunni_rebels.png)](/Sunni_zealots "Sunni zealots") Sunni zealots rise up in revolt and occupy a random province of the country that is _not_ the capital. If the country had chosen the option “He remains our strongest supporter.” of the event ‘[The Khojas](/Tengri_events#tengri_events.17 "Tengri events")’ less then (additionally) 4 times more than the option “Attempt to limit the influence of the Khojas.” then the rebels have size 1, else if the first option was chosen 4 or 5 times more then the rebels have size 2, else if the first option was chosen at least 6 additionally times then the rebels have size 3.

### Mayan\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=26 "Edit section: Mayan") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=26 "Edit section: Mayan")\]

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Codification of the Faith

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_In order to properly spread the traditions and rituals of our people to foreign lands we should create a written account of all religious rules, rituals and laws along with the history of creation. This will allow us to educate even the most ignorant in the proper ways to please the gods._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Mayan.png](/images/thumb/9/98/Mayan.png/28px-Mayan.png)](/Mayan "Mayan") Mayan.
*   owns a province that is _not_ Mayan.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Codified Religious Traditions’_.

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **2** stability.
*   has at least [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **50** [administrative power](/Administrative_power "Administrative power").

If the [![El Dorado.png](/images/thumb/1/16/El_Dorado.png/28px-El_Dorado.png)](/El_Dorado "El Dorado") ‘El Dorado’ DLC is enabled

*   then the country must have reformed its religion
*   else the country must have embraced the [![Renaissance.png](/images/thumb/7/73/Renaissance.png/28px-Renaissance.png)](/Renaissance "Renaissance") [Renaissance](/Renaissance "Renaissance").

* * *

Effects

The country

*   loses [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **50** administrative power.
*   gets the modifier _‘Codified Religious Traditions’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effect:
    *   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+2%** missionary strength.

*   then the country must have reformed its religion
*   else the country must have embraced the [![Renaissance.png](/images/thumb/7/73/Renaissance.png/28px-Renaissance.png)](/Renaissance "Renaissance") [Renaissance](/Renaissance "Renaissance").

### Jewish\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=29 "Edit section: Jewish") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=29 "Edit section: Jewish")\]

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Encourage Conversion to Judaism

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Let us restrict all important offices in the administration of our central, local and military government to members of the true faith while also providing free education in the laws of the Talmud and the Shulkhan Arukh for all lower officials. This way we can encourage that there is both a will and a preparedness to convert._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Jewish.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Jewish.png/28px-Jewish.png)](/Jewish "Jewish") Jewish.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Encouraging Conversion’_.

Allow

[Ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Encouraging Conversion’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+2%** missionary strength,
*   [![Tolerance heathen.png](/images/thumb/d/dc/Tolerance_heathen.png/28px-Tolerance_heathen.png)](/Tolerance_of_heathens "Tolerance of heathens") **−1** tolerance of heathens.

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Build the Third Temple

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.33.

* * *

_For centuries, our people have mourned the loss of the Second Temple and dreamed about its recovery. The time has come. We shall build the Third Temple in Jerusalem again for the glory of the Lord._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   Is [![Jewish.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Jewish.png/28px-Jewish.png)](/Jewish "Jewish") Jewish

Province Jerusalem (379):

*   Does _not_ have province flag third\_temple\_built

Allow

The country:

*   Is [![Jewish.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Jewish.png/28px-Jewish.png)](/Jewish "Jewish") Jewish

Province Jerusalem (379):

*   Is owned by us
*   Is our core
*   Is [![Jewish.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Jewish.png/28px-Jewish.png)](/Jewish "Jewish") Jewish

* * *

Effects

Trigger [![Msg event.png](/images/4/4e/Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event") _“[The Third Temple](/Jewish_events#jewish_flavor.5 "Jewish events")”_ event

* * *

AI will always take this decision, unless it has less than [![Gold Icon.png](/images/2/26/Gold_Icon.png)](/Ducats "Ducats") **6 000** ducats

### Zoroastrian\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=30 "Edit section: Zoroastrian") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=30 "Edit section: Zoroastrian")\]

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Rites of Admission

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Unlike some religions ours do not attempt to force itself upon unknowing children. A Zoroastrian initiation must be done by someone old enough to understand what it entails. Still much could be done to encourage those who do not see the value of our faith._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Zoroastrianism.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Zoroastrianism.png/28px-Zoroastrianism.png)](/Zoroastrian "Zoroastrian") Zoroastrian.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Rites of Admission’_.

Allow

The country:

*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **2** stability.
*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") administrative skill is at least 3.
*   has at least [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **50** [administrative power](/Administrative_power "Administrative power").

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   loses [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **50** administrative power.
*   gets the modifier _‘Rites of Admission’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effect:
    *   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength")**+2%** missionary strength.

id

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Rekindling the Royal Fires

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Of all the fire temples of our faith the legend of the three fires lit by Zoroaster himself are the most prestigious. They have, however, long been lost as our faith declined over the centuries and the locations of the old fires are now unknown. While a fire cannot be recreated we can attempt to find the site of these temples and start new fires to symbolize the rise of our Zoroastrian Empire._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Zoroastrianism.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Zoroastrianism.png/28px-Zoroastrianism.png)](/Zoroastrian "Zoroastrian") Zoroastrian.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Royal Fires’_.

Allow

The country:

*   is an [![Empire rank](/images/thumb/9/9d/Empire.png/28px-Empire.png)](/Government_rank "Empire rank") [empire](/Government_rank "Government rank").
*   owns all of the following [core provinces](/Core_provinces "Core provinces"):
    *   Mashhad (2221), Maragheh (2207), Sabzevar (2235), Bojnord (2236), Shiraz (2218), Khiva (441) and Larestan (2223).

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Royal Fires’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Yearly_prestige "Yearly prestige") **+0.5** yearly prestige,
*   [![Yearly legitimacy.png](/images/thumb/b/bc/Yearly_legitimacy.png/28px-Yearly_legitimacy.png)](/Yearly_legitimacy "Yearly legitimacy") **+0.5** yearly legitimacy,
*   [![Yearly devotion.png](/images/thumb/9/9d/Yearly_devotion.png/28px-Yearly_devotion.png)](/Yearly_devotion "Yearly devotion") **+0.5** yearly devotion,
*   [![Manpower in true faith provinces](/images/thumb/f/f6/Manpower_in_true_faith_provinces.png/28px-Manpower_in_true_faith_provinces.png)](/Manpower "Manpower in true faith provinces") **+20%** Manpower in true faith provinces.

* * *

Map:

Expand

[![Royal Fires map.png](/images/a/a5/Royal_Fires_map.png)](/File:Royal_Fires_map.png)

[](/File:Royal_Fires_map.png "Enlarge")

#### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Zoroastrian Diaspora

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_During the harsh years of oppression in Persia many left their ancestral homes to resettle abroad. The Qissa-i Sanjan tells us of those who took a long and arduous journey to settle in Gujarat and to lit new fires and start anew. Known for their industry these men and women have thrived in their new homeland. Our efforts to make Zoroastrianism the only majority religion within our borders will allow us to reunite with these foreign brothers and sisters._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Zoroastrianism.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Zoroastrianism.png/28px-Zoroastrianism.png)](/Zoroastrian "Zoroastrian") Zoroastrian.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Reunification of the Zoroastrian Diaspora’_.

Allow

The country:

*   owns all of the following [core provinces](/Core_province "Core province"):
    *   Teheran (428), Isfahan (429), Mogostan (431), Kerman (432), Yazd (433), Balkh (450), Thatta (504), Surat (517), Thana (529) and Kirmanshah (2210).
*   owns only provinces that are [![Zoroastrianism.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Zoroastrianism.png/28px-Zoroastrianism.png)](/Zoroastrian "Zoroastrian") Zoroastrian.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _‘Reunification of the Zoroastrian Diaspora’_ until the state religion is changed with the following effects:

*   [![Advisor cost.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Advisor_cost.png/28px-Advisor_cost.png)](/Advisor_costs "Advisor costs") **−10%** advisor cost,
*   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier") **−10%** stability cost modifier,
*   [![Tolerance of the true faith.png](/images/thumb/d/d9/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png/28px-Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png)](/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith "Tolerance of the true faith") **+1** tolerance of the true faith.

* * *

Map:

Expand

[![Zoroastrian Diaspora map.png](/images/thumb/2/21/Zoroastrian_Diaspora_map.png/330px-Zoroastrian_Diaspora_map.png)](/File:Zoroastrian_Diaspora_map.png)

Pirate\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=31 "Edit section: Pirate") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=31 "Edit section: Pirate")\]

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Hoist the Black Flag

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.33.

* * *

_How can laws and civilization compete with freedom and the promise of treasure? It’s time to hoist the black flag and declare a Pirate Republic!_

* * *

[![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century")[![Lions of the North.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Lions_of_the_North.png/28px-Lions_of_the_North.png)](/Lions_of_the_North "Lions of the North")

Available only with the [Golden Century](/Golden_Century "Golden Century") DLC _or_ the [Lions of the North](/Lions_of_the_North "Lions of the North") DLC enabled.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is _not_ a [subject nation](/Subject_nation "Subject nation").
*   is _not_ [the Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State").
*   is _not_ the emperor of the [HRE](/HRE "HRE").
*   is _not_ a revolutionary country.
*   is a [![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/24px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy")monarchy _or_ a [![Government republic.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Government_republic.png/24px-Government_republic.png)](/Republic "Republic")republic.
*   has _not_ enacted [Pirate Republic](/Pirate_Republic "Pirate Republic"), [Presidential Dictator](/Presidential_Dictator "Presidential Dictator"), [Plutocracy (aka Merchant republic)](/Republic#Plutocracy "Republic"), [Dutch Republic](/Dutch_Republic "Dutch Republic"), [Colonial Government](/Colonial_Government "Colonial Government"), [Shogunate](/Shogunate "Shogunate"), [Elective Monarchy](/Elective_Monarchy "Elective Monarchy"), [Celestial Empire](/Celestial_Empire "Celestial Empire"), [Daimyo](/Daimyo "Daimyo"), [American Republic](/American_Republic "American Republic"), [Trading City](/Republic#Trading_City "Republic"), [Free City](/Republic#Free_City "Republic"), [Federal Republic](/Federal_Republic "Federal Republic"), [Veche Republic](/Veche_Republic "Veche Republic") _or_ [Venetian Government](/Venetian_Government "Venetian Government") [government reform](/Government_reform "Government reform").
*   has less than 7 [cities](/Cities "Cities").
*   owns only provinces that are coastal
*   owns only provinces that are [on an island](/Island#province_is_on_an_island "Island") _or_ in [Maghreb](/Maghreb "Maghreb").

Allow

The country:

*   has a [stability](/Stability "Stability") of at least +2.
*   has a navy of at least 90% of the [naval force limit](/Naval_force_limit "Naval force limit").
*   does _not_ have subjects.
*   has at least 10% of the trade power in its [home trade node](/index.php?title=Home_trade_node&action=edit&redlink=1 "Home trade node (page does not exist)") with [privateers](/Privateers "Privateers").
*   is _not_ [bankrupt](/Bankrupt "Bankrupt").
*   is _not_ at [war](/War "War").

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   loses [![Stability.png](/images/thumb/a/ae/Stability.png/24px-Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **2** stability.
*   becomes a [![Government republic.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Government_republic.png/24px-Government_republic.png)](/Republic "Republic")republic.
*   enacts ‘[Pirate Republic](/Pirate_Republic "Pirate Republic")’ government reform.
*   gains [![Republican tradition.png](/images/e/ee/Republican_tradition.png)](/Republic_tradition "Republic tradition") **20** republican tradition.
*   if the country is in the [![Western technology group](/images/thumb/9/95/Western.png/24px-Western.png)](/Technology_group "Western technology group") Western or [![Eastern technology group](/images/thumb/6/6d/Eastern.png/24px-Eastern.png)](/Technology_group "Eastern technology group") Eastern technology groups:
    *   use _New World Pirates Sprites_
*   if the country is in the [![Anatolian technology group](/images/thumb/5/53/Ottoman.png/24px-Ottoman.png)](/Technology_group "Anatolian technology group") Anatolian or [![Muslim technology group](/images/thumb/8/8e/Muslim.png/24px-Muslim.png)](/Technology_group "Muslim technology group") Muslim technology groups:
    *   use _Barbary Pirates Sprites_

  

Religious Conversion\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=32 "Edit section: Religious Conversion") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=32 "Edit section: Religious Conversion")\]

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Embrace the Counter-Reformation

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.32.

* * *

_His Holiness, the Pope, has called for a mighty effort to counter the Protestant movement. With the aid of the newly founded Jesuit order, we shall root out and purge these foul heresies. Apart from more - and more effective missionaries - Protestantism and the Reformed faith shall have a harder time spreading in our realm. (If we ever pick the national ideas 'Ecumenism' or 'Liberté, égalité, fraternité' we will lose this bonus.)_

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Catholicism](/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic") Catholic.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _“Counter-Reformation”_.
*   does _not_ have the idea ‘[Ecumenism](/Ecumenism "Ecumenism")’ (3rd humanist idea).
*   does _not_ have the idea ‘Liberté, Égalité, Fraternité’ (7th idea of [France](/France "France")).

The [![Protestantism](/images/thumb/0/0d/Protestant.png/28px-Protestant.png)](/Protestant "Protestant") [Protestant](/Protestant "Protestant") faith exists for less than 150 years.  
The Counter-Reformation takes place.[\[2\]](#cite_note-2)

Allow

This country:

*   is [![Flag of The Papal State](/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State"), the Holy Roman Emperor _or_ has an [![Opinion.png](/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion") [opinion](/Opinion "Opinion") of at least **\-50** towards [![Flag of The Papal State](/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State").
*   does _not_ have the modifier _“Edict de Nantes”_.[\[3\]](#cite_note-3)

* * *

Effects

If the country is _not_ [![Flag of The Papal State](/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") then:

*    [![Flag of the Papal State](/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") [the Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") gets the opinion modifier _“Embraced Counter-Reformation”_ ([![Opinion.png](/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion") **+75** opinion / **−1** yearly decay / 50 years) towards the country

If the country is _not_ the emperor and the emperor is [![Catholicism](/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic") Catholic then:

*   the emperor gets the opinion modifier _“Embraced Counter-Reformation”_ ([![Opinion.png](/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion") **+75** opinion / **−1** yearly decay / 50 years) towards the country

The country gets the modifier _“Counter-Reformation”_ indefinitely[\[4\]](#cite_note-4) with the following effects:

*   [![Missionary strength vs heretics.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/Missionary_strength_vs_heretics.png/28px-Missionary_strength_vs_heretics.png)](/Missionary_strength_vs_heretics "Missionary strength vs heretics") **+3%** missionary strength vs heretics,
*   [![Papal influence.png](/images/thumb/5/5f/Papal_influence.png/28px-Papal_influence.png)](/Papal_influence "Papal influence") **+0.5** yearly papal influence,
*   [![Missionaries.png](/images/thumb/a/ad/Missionaries.png/28px-Missionaries.png)](/Missionary "Missionary") **+2** missionaries,
*   [![Technology cost.png](/images/thumb/e/ea/Technology_cost.png/28px-Technology_cost.png)](/Technology_cost "Technology cost") **+5%** technology cost,
*   [![Idea cost.png](/images/thumb/3/3c/Idea_cost.png/28px-Idea_cost.png)](/Idea_cost "Idea cost") **+5%** idea cost.

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Kirishitan Conversion

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.32.

* * *

_Since The new Kirishitan religion from Europe has spread so far and wide within our Han, we have considered converting to this new creed. The implications of abandoning the faith of our ancestors are not to be taken lightly._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The [![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven") ‘Mandate of Heaven’ DLC is _not_ enabled.  
The country:

*   has enacted ‘[Daimyo](/Daimyo "Daimyo")’ [government reform](/Government_reform "Government reform").
*   is [![Shintoism](/images/thumb/8/85/Shinto.png/28px-Shinto.png)](/Shinto "Shinto") Shinto.
*   owns a province which is [![Catholicism](/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic") Catholic.

Allow

The country:

*   has [![Catholicism](/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic") Catholic religion as the [dominant religion](/Dominant_religion "Dominant religion").
*   has [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **3** [stability](/Stability "Stability").

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   changes its religion to [![Catholicism](/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic") Catholic.
*   loses [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **4** stability.

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Embrace Islam

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.32.

* * *

_Islam is quickly becoming the dominant religion in Nusantara. We should consider whether the words of the Prophet resonate in our hearts._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   Culture is in Malay group
*   Religion is Dharmic or Eastern
*   is _not_ a [subject nation](/Subject_nation "Subject nation") other than a [tributary state](/Tributary_state "Tributary state").

Allow

The country:

*   [dominant religion](/Dominant_religion "Dominant religion") is [![Sunni Islam](/images/thumb/2/2f/Sunni.png/28px-Sunni.png)](/Sunni "Sunni") Sunni.
*   has at least [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **0** Stability.

* * *

Effects

*   Change religion to [![Sunni Islam](/images/thumb/2/2f/Sunni.png/28px-Sunni.png)](/Sunni "Sunni") Sunni
*   Lose [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** stability
*   Every known [![Sunni Islam](/images/thumb/2/2f/Sunni.png/28px-Sunni.png)](/Sunni "Sunni") Sunni countries with Malay culture:
    *   Gain opinion modifier _“Converted to Islam”_ ([![Opinion.png](/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion") **+50** opinion / **−2** yearly decay) towards the country

Trade\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=33 "Edit section: Trade") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=33 "Edit section: Trade")\]
