### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Confirm Thalassocracy

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_By confirming our Thalassocracy, our rule by the sea, we will receive tremendous bonuses to our navy, propelling us into a position of unrivaled dominance over the oceans._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   does _not_ have the modifier _“Thalassocracy”_.
*   is the strongest trade power in one of the following [trade nodes](/Trade_node "Trade node"):
    *   Genoa, Venice, Tunis, Ragusa, Alexandria, Lübeck, Baltic Sea, English Channel, North Sea, Novgorod, Goa, Gulf of Aden, Indus, Ceylon, Bengal _or_ Malacca.

Allow

The country:

*   has completed the [![Maritime idea group.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Maritime_idea_group.png/28px-Maritime_idea_group.png)](/Maritime_ideas "Maritime ideas") [Maritime idea group](/Maritime_idea_group "Maritime idea group").
*   is the strongest trade power:
    *   in Genoa, Venice, Tunis, Ragusa and Alexandria _or_
    *   in Lübeck, Baltic Sea, English Channel, North Sea and Novgorod _or_
    *   in Goa, Gulf of Aden, Indus, Ceylon, Bengal and Malacca.

* * *

Effects

The country gets the modifier _“Thalassocracy”_ for the rest of the campaign with the following effects:

*   [![Yearly navy tradition.png](/images/thumb/d/dc/Yearly_navy_tradition.png/28px-Yearly_navy_tradition.png)](/Yearly_navy_tradition "Yearly navy tradition") **+0.25** yearly navy tradition,
*   [![Light ship cost.png](/images/thumb/d/de/Light_ship_cost.png/28px-Light_ship_cost.png)](/Light_ship_cost "Light ship cost") **−10%** light ship cost,
*   [![Merchants.png](/images/thumb/2/24/Merchants.png/28px-Merchants.png)](/Merchant "Merchant") **+1** merchants,
*   [![Diplomatic technology cost](/images/thumb/e/e1/Diplomatic_technology_cost.png/28px-Diplomatic_technology_cost.png)](/Technology_cost "Diplomatic technology cost") **−5%** diplomatic technology cost.

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Close Foreign Trade

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Minimize Western influences by restricting the number of trading posts that are allowed to be operated by foreign traders and promote stricter rules for foreign trade and missionary work over all._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is in the [![Chinese technology group](/images/thumb/3/37/Chinese.png/28px-Chinese.png)](/Technology_group "Chinese technology group") Chinese technology group.
*   has at least 1 home port.
*   does _not_ have the modifier _“Condemn Western Influences”_.

Any known country within the [![Western technology group](/images/thumb/9/95/Western.png/28px-Western.png)](/Technology_group "Western technology group") Western technology group is the strongest trade power of a trade node in [South](/South_China "South China") _or_ [North China](/North_China "North China") and has a [merchant](/Merchant "Merchant") there.

Allow

The country:

*   [ruler](/Ruler "Ruler")'s [![Military power.png](/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power") military skill is at least 3.

Any known country:

*   is in the [![Western technology group](/images/thumb/9/95/Western.png/28px-Western.png)](/Technology_group "Western technology group") Western technology group.
*   is the strongest trade power of a trade node in [South](/South_China "South China") _or_ [North China](/North_China "North China") and has a [merchant](/Merchant "Merchant") there.
*   has an [![Opinion.png](/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion") opinion of less than **\-100** towards the country.

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   gains [![Mercantilism.png](/images/thumb/0/05/Mercantilism.png/28px-Mercantilism.png)](/Mercantilism "Mercantilism") **5%** mercantilism.
*   gets the modifier _“Increased Narrow-minded”_ for [![Time Icon.png](/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time") 10 years with the following effects:
    *   [![Technology cost.png](/images/thumb/e/ea/Technology_cost.png/28px-Technology_cost.png)](/Technology_cost "Technology cost") **+5%** technology cost,
    *   [![Missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Missionary_strength.png/28px-Missionary_strength.png)](/Missionary_strength "Missionary strength") **+1%** missionary strength.
*   gets the modifier _“Condemn Western Influences”_ for the rest of the campaign with the following effects:
    *   [![Trade efficiency.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Trade_efficiency.png/28px-Trade_efficiency.png)](/Trade_efficiency "Trade efficiency") **−8%** trade efficiency,
    *   [![Stability cost modifier.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Stability_cost_modifier.png/28px-Stability_cost_modifier.png)](/Stability_cost_modifier "Stability cost modifier") **−6%** stability cost modifier,
    *   [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Yearly_prestige "Yearly prestige") **+0.5** yearly prestige.

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Stop Foreign Slave Trade

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_For too long we have been granting European traders access to our markets. Slavery has brought some regions of our country to it's knees as many young men are shipped across the Atlantic. A trade that it is now clear is no longer in our interest. Let us break these bands and displace those who would profit from our loss!_

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   has the modifier _“[Slaving Economy](/Institution_events#Slave_Traders "Institution events")”_.

Allow

The country:

*   has embraced [![Feudalism.png](/images/thumb/e/e8/Feudalism.png/28px-Feudalism.png)](/Feudalism "Feudalism") [feudalism](/Feudalism "Feudalism") and [![Colonialism](/images/thumb/4/49/Colonialism.png/28px-Colonialism.png)](/Institutions#Colonialism "Colonialism") [colonialism](/Institutions#Colonialism "Institutions").
*   has an [![Administrative technology.png](/images/8/8e/Administrative_technology.png)](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology") [administrative technology](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology") of at least level 12.
*   is _not_ [tribal](/Government#Tribal_governments "Government").
*   has at least [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power")**200** [administrative power](/Administrative_power "Administrative power").

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   loses [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **200** administrative power.
*   loses the modifier _“Slaving Economy”_.

If a province of the country has the modifier _“Major Slave Market”_ then that province:

*   loses the modifier _“Major Slave Market”_.
*   loses its current [trade good](/Trade_good "Trade good").

_Local Strongmen in provinces with Slave Trade as their main source of income will attempt to sidestep this edict for 15 years._  

Every province of the country with [slaves](/Slaves "Slaves") as trade good:

*   get the modifier _“Slaver Chiefs”_ for 15 years with the following effects:
    *   [![Local autonomy.png](/images/thumb/1/17/Local_autonomy.png/28px-Local_autonomy.png)](/Local_autonomy "Local autonomy") **+0.05** monthly autonomy change,
    *   [![Local unrest.png](/images/thumb/d/dd/Local_unrest.png/28px-Local_unrest.png)](/Local_unrest "Local unrest") **+4** local unrest.

### Trade goods\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=34 "Edit section: Trade goods") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=34 "Edit section: Trade goods")\]

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Grow Cloves in Zanzibar

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_We have found that cloves, a valuable trade good currently found only in the Spice Islands, can be grown on the island of Zanzibar off the coast of Africa._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   Owns any province producing [![Cloves.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Cloves.png/28px-Cloves.png)](/Cloves "Cloves") Cloves
*   Is _not_ [![Indian technology group](/images/thumb/1/19/Indian.png/28px-Indian.png)](/Technology_group "Indian technology group") Indian, [![Chinese technology group](/images/thumb/3/37/Chinese.png/28px-Chinese.png)](/Technology_group "Chinese technology group") Chinese _or_ [![Aboriginal technology group](/images/thumb/5/56/Aboriginal.png/28px-Aboriginal.png)](/Technology_group "Aboriginal technology group") Aboriginal
*   Province Zanzibar does _not_ produce [![Cloves.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Cloves.png/28px-Cloves.png)](/Cloves "Cloves") Cloves

Allow

The country:

*   Owns any province producing [![Cloves.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Cloves.png/28px-Cloves.png)](/Cloves "Cloves") Cloves
*   Owns province Zanzibar

* * *

Effects

Province Zanzibar:

*   Change province's goods produced to [![Cloves.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Cloves.png/28px-Cloves.png)](/Cloves "Cloves") Cloves

This section lists [decisions](/Decisions "Decisions") that were converted from old-style missions in [patch 1.25](/Patch_1.25 "Patch 1.25"). They are all [easter eggs](/Easter_eggs "Easter eggs") based on puns.

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Become King of Gonder

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_It is Aragon's Destiny to become King of Gonder. Now that we have finally figured out where it is we should do something about this. Make Gonder Aragon's as we cannot escape our destiny._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   is [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon").
*   does _not_ have the modifier _‘Inspiring Victory’_.
*   is _not_ a [subject nation](/Subject_nation "Subject nation") other than a [tributary state](/Tributary_state "Tributary state").
*   owns at least 1 province in [Egypt (region)](/Egypt_(region) "Egypt (region)") or the [Horn of Africa](/Horn_of_Africa "Horn of Africa").
*   has discovered Gonder (1224) that:
    *   does _not_ have the modifier _‘City of the Kings’_.
    *   is _not_ owned by an ally, a subject or the overlord of [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon").

Allow

 [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon"):

*   owns its [core province](/Core_province "Core province") Gonder (1224).

* * *

Effects

 [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon"):

*   gets the modifier _‘Inspiring Victory’_ for [![Time Icon.png](/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time") 10 years, giving the following effects:
    *   [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige") **+1** yearly prestige,
    *   [![Manpower recovery speed.png](/images/thumb/e/ee/Manpower_recovery_speed.png/28px-Manpower_recovery_speed.png)](/Manpower_recovery_speed "Manpower recovery speed") **+10%** manpower recovery speed.

Gonder (1224):

*   gets the modifier _‘City of the Kings’_ until its owner changes, giving the following effects:
    *   [![Local defensiveness.png](/images/thumb/1/15/Local_defensiveness.png/28px-Local_defensiveness.png)](/Local_defensiveness "Local defensiveness") **+25%** local defensiveness,
    *   [![Local manpower modifier.png](/images/thumb/8/8b/Local_manpower_modifier.png/28px-Local_manpower_modifier.png)](/Local_manpower_modifier "Local manpower modifier") **+10%** local manpower modifier.

* * *

AI will not take this decision.

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Recover our Cultural Heritage

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_Legends speak of a Japanese artist who fled to a distant land after incurring the wrath of the Emperor. He brought with him his most prized possessions: Picture-books chronicling the history of a 'higher' school where the most legendary Samurai of his age were educated. We believe that this lost cultural treasure lies hidden somewhere in the jungles of Africa, and it is our duty to recover it!_

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   has its [primary culture](/Primary_culture "Primary culture") from the Japanese culture group.
*   is _not_ a [subject nation](/Subject_nation "Subject nation") other than a [tributary state](/Tributary_state "Tributary state").
*   owns at least 20 [cities](/Cities "Cities").
*   has at least 1 [home port](/Home_port "Home port").
*   has its [capital](/Capital "Capital") in [Japan (region)](/Japan_(region) "Japan (region)").
*   owns a province in [Africa](/Africa "Africa").
*   has discovered Manga (2284) that:
    *   has _not_ been affected by this event so far.
    *   is _not_ owned by an ally, a subject or the overlord this country.

Plays with normal or historical nations.

Allow

The country:

*   owns its [core province](/Core_province "Core province") Manga (2284).

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   gets the modifier _‘Inspiring Victory’_ for 10 years, giving the following effects:
    *   [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige") **+1** yearly prestige,
    *   [![Manpower recovery speed.png](/images/thumb/e/ee/Manpower_recovery_speed.png/28px-Manpower_recovery_speed.png)](/Manpower_recovery_speed "Manpower recovery speed") **+10%** manpower recovery speed.

Manga (2284):

*   changes its [trade good](/Trade_good "Trade good") to [![Paper.png](/images/thumb/b/b2/Paper.png/28px-Paper.png)](/Paper "Paper") paper.

* * *

AI will not take this decision.

The year is before 1500.

*   set country flag shadow\_kingdom\_early\_success
*   Every country that has not been reined in may leave the Empire! (gets _The Shadow Kingdom_ event)

As the peasants enforce their demands or create new republics, they come closer to enforcing their demands. But when a new republic is crushed, the tide turns in favour of the nobility._

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Mass Revolutionary Guard Training

_The enemies of our Revolution is many, we need to make sure we are prepared to repel the threat that lurks beyond our borders and that we have many loyal troops to fight for us._

*   Gain country modifier _“Mass Revolutionary Guard Recruitment”_ for the rest of the game, giving the following effects:
    *   [![Special unit force limit.png](/images/thumb/0/0e/Special_unit_force_limit.png/28px-Special_unit_force_limit.png)](/Special_unit_force_limit "Special unit force limit") **+10%** Special unit force limit

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Professional Revolutionary Guard Training

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

* * *

_The Guard comes from all the corners of our nation. They are put through rigorous training before being sent to the field to keep the standard of our army high._

* * *

[![Cradle of Civilization.png](/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization")

Available only with the [Cradle of Civilization](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") DLC enabled.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   Is [revolutionary](/Revolutionary "Revolutionary")
*   Does _not_ have country modifier_“Professional Revolutionary Guard Training”_

Allow

The country:

*   Is revolutionary
*   Has at least [![Army professionalism.png](/images/thumb/6/64/Army_professionalism.png/28px-Army_professionalism.png)](/Army_professionalism "Army professionalism") **40%** Army professionalism

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   Gains country modifier _“Professional Revolutionary Guard Training”_ for the rest of the game, giving the following effects:
    *   allows [Revolutionary Guard](/Army#Revolutionary_Guard "Army") recruitment
    *   [![Army drill decay modifier.png](/images/thumb/6/62/Army_drill_decay_modifier.png/28px-Army_drill_decay_modifier.png)](/Regiment_drill_loss "Regiment drill loss") **−25%** Regiment drill loss
    *   [![Land maintenance modifier.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Land_maintenance_modifier.png/28px-Land_maintenance_modifier.png)](/Land_maintenance_modifier "Land maintenance modifier") **+50%** Land maintenance modifier

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Vanguard Revolutionary Guard Training

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_The Guard have the most zealous of our citizenry. They fight first in a battle and leave last, because of their vanguard nature they must be equiped and trained to be able to sustain the most heavy fighting._

* * *

[![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor")

Available only with the [Emperor](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor (DLC)") DLC enabled.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

The country:

*   Is [revolutionary](/Revolutionary "Revolutionary")
*   Does _not_ have country modifier _“Vanguard Revolutionary Guard Training”_

Allow

The country:

*   Is revolutionary
*   If DLC [![Cradle of Civilization.png](/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") Cradle of Civilization is active
    *   has at least [![Army professionalism.png](/images/thumb/6/64/Army_professionalism.png/28px-Army_professionalism.png)](/Army_professionalism "Army professionalism") **60%** Army professionalism

* * *

Effects

The country:

*   Gains country modifier _“Vanguard Revolutionary Guard Training”_ for the rest of the game, giving the following effects:
    *   allows [Revolutionary Guard](/Army#Revolutionary_Guard "Army") recruitment
    *   [![Shock damage received.png](/images/thumb/3/36/Shock_damage_received.png/28px-Shock_damage_received.png)](/Shock_damage_received "Shock damage received") **−10%** Shock damage received
    *   [![Fire damage received.png](/images/thumb/e/e7/Fire_damage_received.png/28px-Fire_damage_received.png)](/Fire_damage_received "Fire damage received") **−10%** Fire damage received
    *   [![Land maintenance modifier.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Land_maintenance_modifier.png/28px-Land_maintenance_modifier.png)](/Land_maintenance_modifier "Land maintenance modifier") **+50%** Land maintenance modifier

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Curtail the Prussian Confederation

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.31.

* * *

_We must put an end to the Prussian Confederation lest the situation spiral out of control. We must decide whether appeasement or repression is the right path._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   Has had the [![Msg event.png](/images/thumb/4/4e/Msg_event.png/20px-Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event") event _"[The Prussian Confederation Revolts|](/Teutonic_events#flavor_teu.1 "Teutonic events")"_
*   Has _not_ had the [![Msg event.png](/images/thumb/4/4e/Msg_event.png/20px-Msg_event.png)](/Event "Event") event _"[The Prussian Confederation|](/Teutonic_events#flavor_teu.4 "Teutonic events")"_
*   Has _not_ enacted this decision before
*   Has _not_ the _“Concede to the Prussian Confederation”_ estate privilege

[![Time Icon.png](/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time") The year is before 1500.

Allow

*   [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") Stability is at least **+1**
*   No province is controlled by rebels
*   No [![Particularist rebels.png](/images/thumb/8/85/Particularist_rebels.png/28px-Particularist_rebels.png)](/Particularists "Particularists") Particularist rebels have risen in revolt
*   If [![Burghers.png](/images/thumb/d/dd/Burghers.png/28px-Burghers.png)](/Burghers "Burghers") Burghers estate does _not_ exist
    *   [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige") Prestige is at least **+1**
*   Else, has at least [![Crownland.png](/images/thumb/e/ed/Crownland.png/28px-Crownland.png)](/Crown_land "Crown land") **40%** [crown land](/Crown_land "Crown land") ownership

* * *

Effects

*   Gain [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige") **10** prestige
*   Gain country modifier _“Curtailed the Prussian Confederation”_ for [![Time Icon.png](/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time") 20 years, giving the following effect:
    *   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") **−1** National unrest

    *   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture is Hakka
    *   Is _not_ owned by [![Flag of Ming](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ming.png/20px-Ming.png)](/Ming "Ming") [Ming](/Ming "Ming")

    *   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture is Hakka
    *   Religion is [![Confucianism](/images/thumb/a/a2/Confucianism.png/28px-Confucianism.png)](/Confucian "Confucian") Confucian

    *   Enact government reform [Kongsi Federation](/Kongsi_Federation "Kongsi Federation")
    *   Remove all provinces from the Holy Roman Empire, unless an elector or the Emperor
    *   Province Pontianak (4802) becomes the new [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") capital. If it was in the empire and the country isn't, it is removed from the empire.
    *   Trigger country event _“[New Traditions & Ambitions](/Idea_group_events#ideagroups.1 "Idea group events")”_ if it doesn't have [![Lanfang.png](/images/thumb/c/c9/Lanfang.png/20px-Lanfang.png)](/File:Lanfang.png) Lanfang Ideas

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)The Fate of Joan of Arc

![Ambox outdated info.png](https://central.paradoxwikis.com/images/thumb/6/65/Ambox_outdated_info.png/22px-Ambox_outdated_info.png)

Please help with verifying or updating this infobox. It was last verified for [version](/Europa_Universalis_4_Wiki:Versioning "Europa Universalis 4 Wiki:Versioning") 1.32.

* * *

_Joan of Arc turned the tide of the Hundred Year's War by saving Orléans and having King Charles crowned in Reims. We could make good use of her as a national symbol but first we need to clear her name of allegations of witchcraft and heresy._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   Global flag retrial\_of\_joan\_of\_arc is _not_ set
*   Culture is in French group
*   Religion is [![Catholicism](/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic") Catholic
*   Orleanais (184) is owned by the country or its non-tributary subjects
*   It is currently the [![Age of Discovery.png](/images/thumb/e/eb/Age_of_Discovery.png/28px-Age_of_Discovery.png)](/Age_of_Discovery "Age of Discovery") Age of Discovery

Allow

*   Paris (183), Caux (167) and Barrois (187) are owned by the country or its non-tributary subjects
*   All provinces in the France region, excluding Calais (87):
    *   Are _not_ owned by [![Flag of England](/images/thumb/2/21/England.png/20px-England.png)](/England "England") [England](/England "England") _or_ [![Flag of Great Britain](/images/thumb/2/2b/Great_Britain.png/20px-Great_Britain.png)](/Great_Britain "Great Britain") [Great Britain](/Great_Britain "Great Britain")
*   At least one of:
    *    [![Flag of The Papal State](/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") has at least [![Opinion.png](/images/thumb/9/97/Opinion.png/24px-Opinion.png)](/Opinion "Opinion") **+100** opinion towards us
    *   Is the Curia controller

* * *

Effects

*   Trigger country event _“[The Retrial of Joan of Arc](/Orleans_events#flavor_orl.4 "Orleans events")”_
*   Set global flag retrial\_of\_joan\_of\_arc

    *   Is open for colonization

Target province:

AI will always take this decision.

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Provoke Hanseatic Trade Conflict

_The Hansa have the pesky trait to be difficult to deal with. They compete with our trade dominance in the Baltic Sea, and their position within the Holy Roman Empire grants them protection from us._

However, the Emperor is only obliged to support the Hansa in a defensive war. By provoking the Hansa into attacking us we can ensure the dismantling of the Hanseatic League without having to wage war with the entirety of the Holy Roman Empire. All we need to do is to provoke the merchants of the Hansa...

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   Country flag dan\_enable\_trade\_conflict\_war\_decision is set
*   Has the mission _“The Cities of the Hansa”_
*   None of:
    *   Has completed the mission _“The Cities of the Hansa”_

Allow

*   At least 3 of the following are true:
    *   Province Stralsund (47):
        *   Province owner:
            *   At least one of:
                *   Our country
                    *   The country has the Trade Conflict [casus belli](/Casus_belli "Casus belli") against Previously mentioned country
                *   The country is embargoed by Our country
    *   Province Stettin (1858):
        *   Province owner:
            *   At least one of:
                *   Our country
                    *   The country has the Trade Conflict [casus belli](/Casus_belli "Casus belli") against Previously mentioned country
                *   The country is embargoed by Our country
    *   Province Lübeck (45):
        *   Province owner:
            *   At least one of:
                *   Our country
                    *   The country has the Trade Conflict [casus belli](/Casus_belli "Casus belli") against Previously mentioned country
                *   The country is embargoed by Our country
    *   Province Hamburg (44):
        *   Province owner:
            *   At least one of:
                *   Our country
                    *   The country has the Trade Conflict [casus belli](/Casus_belli "Casus belli") against Previously mentioned country
                *   The country is embargoed by Our country
    *   Province Bremen (1874):
        *   Province owner:
            *   At least one of:
                *   Our country
                    *   The country has the Trade Conflict [casus belli](/Casus_belli "Casus belli") against Previously mentioned country
                *   The country is embargoed by Our country

* * *

Effects

*   Clear country flag dan\_enable\_trade\_conflict\_war\_decision
*   _Tooltip: “The owners of \[47.GetName\], \[1858.GetName\], \[45.GetName\], \[44.GetName\] and \[1874.GetName\] will (if they are not \[Root.GetName\] or a \[Root.GetAdjective\] subject) either declare War on \[Root.GetName\] with the Trade Conflict casus belli, or they will submit to \[Root.GetAdjective\] Trade Dominance.  
      
    Trade League leaders will call ALL members of their respective league into the war.”_
*   Hidden effect:
    *   If:
        *   Limited to:
            *   None of:
                *   Stralsund (47) is owned by the country or or its non-tributary subjects
        *   Province Stralsund (47):
            *   Province owner:
                *   Trigger country event _“Raise of the Sound Toll”_
    *   If:
        *   Limited to:
            *   None of:
                *   Stettin (1858) is owned by the country or or its non-tributary subjects
        *   Province Stettin (1858):
            *   Province owner:
                *   Trigger country event _“Raise of the Sound Toll”_
    *   If:
        *   Limited to:
            *   None of:
                *   Lübeck (45) is owned by the country or or its non-tributary subjects
        *   Province Lübeck (45):
            *   Province owner:
                *   Trigger country event _“Raise of the Sound Toll”_
    *   If:
        *   Limited to:
            *   None of:
                *   Hamburg (44) is owned by the country or or its non-tributary subjects
        *   Province Hamburg (44):
            *   Province owner:
                *   Trigger country event _“Raise of the Sound Toll”_
    *   If:
        *   Limited to:
            *   None of:

In a polytheistic religion such as ours, the choice to devote oneself to only one of the many splendid gods is not easily taken, and most often one will reconsider their choice as their life progresses in unthought ways. Fortunately, our priests commune with gods, and allow our \[Root.Monarch.GetTitle\] to change their personal deity.

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Proclaim Protection for the Protestants

_The Protestants of the Holy Roman Empire are victims of inquisitions, open hostility and discrimination by the Imperial Crown itself. But they lack the courage and the strength to call to arms and defend themselves against the injustice done to them._

It is time for us to side with the Reformation, and proclam officially that we will support and protect the Protestants of the Holy Roman Empire.

* * *

Expand

*   The Peace of Westphalia has _not_ been signed

*   [![Imperial authority.png](/images/thumb/4/46/Imperial_authority.png/28px-Imperial_authority.png)](/Imperial_authority "Imperial authority") Holy Roman Empire exists

Maybe a purchase of the island from \[369.Owner.GetName\] might be possible.

        *   Is _not_ at war

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Enforce the Hangul Alphabet

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   Has government type where: Has Hangul Alphabet decisions.
*   None of:
    *   Has country modifier _“Enforced the Hangul Alphabet”_

    *   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") **+1** National unrest
*   _Tooltip: “Can only be enforced or revoked once per ruler lifetime.”_

    *   (unrecognized string “max hostile attrition” for [Template:Icon](/Template:Icon "Template:Icon")) **+3** Max hostile attrition
*   _Tooltip: “Enables the recruitment of the Righteous Army mercenary company during Defensive Wars.

* * *

Effects

*   Pay [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **100** Administrative power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)
*   Pay [![Diplomatic power.png](/images/d/da/Diplomatic_power.png)](/Diplomatic_power "Diplomatic power") **100** Diplomatic power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)
*   Pay [![Military power.png](/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power") **100** Military power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)
*   Lose [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **3** stability
*   Trigger country event _“Negotiations with the Janissaries”_

* * *

AI decision factors:

*   Base weight: 1

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   The country has a parliament
*   Has government type where: Has the English Parliament
*   Has unlocked the [![Parliament.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Parliament.png/28px-Parliament.png)](/Parliament "Parliament") parliament issue _“Acts of High Admiralty”_
*   Has not enacted the [![Parliament.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Parliament.png/28px-Parliament.png)](/Parliament "Parliament") parliament issue _“Acts of High Admiralty”_

Allow

*   Doesn't have an ongoing [debate](/Debate "Debate") in [parliament](/Parliament "Parliament")

* * *

*   Start a debate on _“Acts of High Admiralty”_ in [![Parliament.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Parliament.png/28px-Parliament.png)](/Parliament "Parliament") parliament
*   _Tooltip: “Bribes are 100% more expensive for this Parliament Issue”_
*   _Tooltip: “The issue has the following effects if successfully passed:”_
*   _The game displays a tooltip block without any actual effects in this place_

### from RestoreColorORName.txt\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=64 "Edit section: from RestoreColorORName.txt") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=64 "Edit section: from RestoreColorORName.txt")\]

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Restore Our Name

_This National Decision allows for the restoration of our proper current name._

It will be available for 10 years after adopting a new name.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   Country flag has\_overriden\_name\_flag is set
*   At least one of:
    *   Country flag has\_eyalet\_country\_name is set
    *   None of:
        *   Has had country flag has\_overriden\_name\_flag for at least 10 years

Allow

*   At least one of:
    *   Is player-controlled
    *   Is _not_ a subject nation
*   Is _not_ at war

* * *

Effects

*   Restore the country name to its default value
*   Clear country flag has\_overriden\_name\_flag
*   Clear country flag has\_eyalet\_country\_name

* * *

AI decision factors:

*   Base weight: 100
*   Base weight \* **0** if the following are true:
    *   None of:
        *   Country flag has\_eyalet\_country\_name is set

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Restore our Color

_This National Decision allows for the restoration of our proper current color._

It will be available for 10 years after adopting a new name.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   Country flag has\_overriden\_color\_flag is set
*   At least one of:
    *   None of:
        *   Has had country flag has\_overriden\_color\_flag for at least 10 years
    *   Country flag has\_eyalet\_color is set

Allow

*   Is _not_ a subject nation
*   Is _not_ at war

* * *

Effects

*   restore\_country\_color = yes
    
*   Clear country flag has\_overriden\_color\_flag
*   Clear country flag has\_eyalet\_color

* * *

AI decision factors:

*   Base weight: 100

### from Russia.txt\[[edit](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&veaction=edit&section=65 "Edit section: from Russia.txt") | [edit source](/index.php?title=List_of_decision_lists&action=edit&section=65 "Edit section: from Russia.txt")\]

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Promote Vodka Sales

_The masses start to become uneasy. A promoted sale of our vodka products might improve the mood of our people._

Or at least redirect their aggression towards each other.

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   Country flag rus\_enable\_vodka\_sales\_decision is set

Allow

*   Country has at least 1 province producing [![Grain.png](/images/thumb/6/66/Grain.png/28px-Grain.png)](/Grain "Grain") Grain
*   At least one of:
    *   None of:
        *   Country flag rus\_sold\_vodka\_to\_the\_people is set
    *   Has had country flag rus\_sold\_vodka\_to\_the\_people for at least 10 years

* * *

Effects

*   Clear country flag rus\_sold\_vodka\_to\_the\_people
*   Set country flag rus\_sold\_vodka\_to\_the\_people
*   add\_rebel\_progress
    
    *   value = -20
        
*   Gain **6** years of production income from provinces which fulfill the following conditions:
    *   Produces [![Grain.png](/images/thumb/6/66/Grain.png/28px-Grain.png)](/Grain "Grain") Grain
*   _Tooltip: “Every owned Grain province loses 10 Prosperity.”_
*   Hidden effect:
    *   Every owned province:
        *   Limited to:
            *   Produces [![Grain.png](/images/thumb/6/66/Grain.png/28px-Grain.png)](/Grain "Grain") Grain
        *   Lose [![Prosperity icon m.png](/images/thumb/6/60/Prosperity_icon_m.png/28px-Prosperity_icon_m.png)](/Prosperity "Prosperity") **10** progress towards prosperity
*   If:
    *   Limited to:
        *   Has country modifier _“Vodka Sales”_
    *   extend\_country\_modifier
        
        *   name = rus\_vodka\_sales
            
        *   duration = 3650
            
*   Else:
    *   Gain country modifier _“Vodka Sales”_ for 20 years, giving the following effects:
        *   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") **−1** National unrest
        *   [![Institution spread.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Institution_spread.png/28px-Institution_spread.png)](/Institution_spread "Institution spread") **−33%** Institution spread

* * *

AI decision factors:

*   Base weight: 1

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Abolish the Serfdom

_The serfdom had its use, but now it is hindering us to advance to a new, industrialized era. The peasantry needs to be freed from the maws of the Nobles and the Burghers._

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   Country flag final\_serfdom\_privileges is set

Allow

*   [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") Stability is at least **+1**
*   Pay [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **100** Administrative power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)
*   Pay [![Diplomatic power.png](/images/d/da/Diplomatic_power.png)](/Diplomatic_power "Diplomatic power") **100** Diplomatic power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)
*   Pay [![Military power.png](/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power") **100** Military power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)

* * *

Effects

*   Clear country flag final\_serfdom\_privileges
*   Lose [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") **1** stability
*   Pay [![Administrative power.png](/images/e/ef/Administrative_power.png)](/Administrative_power "Administrative power") **100** Administrative power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)
*   Pay [![Diplomatic power.png](/images/d/da/Diplomatic_power.png)](/Diplomatic_power "Diplomatic power") **100** Diplomatic power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)
*   Pay [![Military power.png](/images/9/98/Military_power.png)](/Military_power "Military power") **100** Military power[\[7\]](#cite_note-allpowercost-7)
*   Remove the estate privilege _“Total Serfdom”_
*   Remove the estate privilege _“Restricted Serfdom”_
*   Remove the estate privilege _“Devastating Serfdom”_
*   One random owned province:
    *   [![Noble rebels.png](/images/thumb/4/42/Noble_rebels.png/28px-Noble_rebels.png)](/Noble_rebels "Noble rebels") Noble rebels (size 3) rise in revolt

* * *

AI decision factors:

*   Base weight: 1

id

### ![Execute decision.png](/images/6/6d/Execute_decision.png)Proclaim the Emperor Title

_For far too long the other powers of \[Root.Capital.GetContinentName\] have considered us as weak. Not worth the attention on the stage which is the world._

We must show them that we are no backwater, rundown principality but a proper Empire. We must demonstrate our power through strength and superiority!

* * *

Expand 

Potential requirements

*   DLC [![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination") Domination is active
*   Is [![Flag of Russia](/images/thumb/e/ee/Russia.png/20px-Russia.png)](/Russia "Russia") [Russia](/Russia "Russia")
*   None of:
    *   Country flag rus\_proclaimed\_empire\_title is set

Allow

*   If:
    *   Limited to:
        *   At least one of:
            *   DLC [![Rights of Man.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Rights_of_Man.png/28px-Rights_of_Man.png)](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man") Rights of Man is active
            *   DLC [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor") Emperor is active
    *   Is a [great power](/Great_power "Great power")
*   Else:
    *   Country's total [![Development.png](/images/thumb/a/a4/Development.png/28px-Development.png)](/Development "Development") development is at least 1 000
*   Has at least 90 _“Modernization”_ in _“Modernization Mechanic”_
*   At least one of:
    *   Any known country:
        *   At least one of:
            *   Our country is a rival
            *   Our country is viewed as an enemy
        *   Has been humiliated by Our country
    *   None of:
        *   At least 1 of the following are true:
            *   All discovered countries:
                *   At least one of:
                    *   Our country is a rival
                    *   Our country is viewed as an enemy

* * *

Effects

*   Set country flag rus\_proclaimed\_empire\_title
*   Trigger country event _“Formation of the \[Root.GetAdjective\] Empire”_

* * *

AI decision factors:

*   Base weight: 1

1.  [↑](#cite_ref-1 "Jump up") The country has chosen the option “\[Root.Heir.GetName\] will be happy to learn of their god.” of the event [Missions in \[Root.Capital.GetCapitalName\]](/Shinto_events#shinto_events.39 "Shinto events") for its current heir.
2.  [↑](#cite_ref-2 "Jump up") I.e. the global flag ‘counter\_reformation’ is set. This flag is set by the event [The Council of $PROVINCECAPITAL$](/Catholic_events#The_Council_of_.24PROVINCECAPITAL.24 "Catholic events") or when the scenario starts on 1545.12.13 or later.
3.  [↑](#cite_ref-3 "Jump up") The modifier _“Edict de Nantes”_ is set by the French decision [Enact Edict de Nantes](/France#Enact_Edict_de_Nantes "France") and removed by the French decision [Revoke Edict de Nantes](/France#Revoke_Edict_de_Nantes "France").
4.  [↑](#cite_ref-4 "Jump up") The modifier _“Counter-Reformation”_ is removed by the following events:
    
    *   ‘[The Counter-Reformation Ends](/Religious_events#The_Counter-Reformation_Ends_2 "Religious events")’, if the country is _not_ Catholic anymore.
    *   ‘[The Counter-Reformation Ends](/Religious_events#The_Counter-Reformation_Ends_3 "Religious events")’, if the Protestant religion exist longer than 150 years.
    *   ‘[The Counter-Reformation Ends](/Religious_events#The_Counter-Reformation_Ends_4 "Religious events")’, if France has the idea ‘Liberté, Égalité, Fraternité’.
    *   ‘[The Counter-Reformation Ends](/Religious_events#The_Counter-Reformation_Ends_5 "Religious events")’, if the country has the idea ‘Ecumenism’.
    *   ‘[The King of the Jesuits](/Polish_events#The_King_of_the_Jesuits "Polish events")’ – option “Religious Freedom won the day”.
    
5.  [↑](#cite_ref-5 "Jump up") bug
6.  ↑ [Jump up to: 6.0](#cite_ref-siberian_colony_6-0) [6.1](#cite_ref-siberian_colony_6-1) Only if uncolonized. Age ability "[Higher Developed Colonies](/Ages#Abilities "Ages")" applies.  
    Else, if owned by us,
    
    *   Gain [![Base tax.png](/images/9/90/Base_tax.png)](/Base_tax "Base tax") **1** base tax
    *   Gain [![Production.png](/images/thumb/a/ad/Production.png/28px-Production.png)](/Production "Production") **1** base production
    *   Gain [![Manpower.png](/images/thumb/0/0c/Manpower.png/28px-Manpower.png)](/Manpower "Manpower") **1** base manpower
    
    Otherwise, gain a [permanent claim](/Permanent_claim "Permanent claim").
7.  ↑ [Jump up to: 7.00](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-0) [7.01](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-1) [7.02](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-2) [7.03](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-3) [7.04](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-4) [7.05](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-5) [7.06](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-6) [7.07](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-7) [7.08](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-8) [7.09](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-9) [7.10](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-10) [7.11](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-11) [7.12](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-12) [7.13](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-13) [7.14](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-14) [7.15](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-15) [7.16](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-16) [7.17](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-17) [7.18](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-18) [7.19](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-19) [7.20](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-20) [7.21](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-21) [7.22](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-22) [7.23](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-23) [7.24](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-24) [7.25](#cite_ref-allpowercost_7-25) This cost is modified by the [![All power costs.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/All_power_costs.png/28px-All_power_costs.png)](/All_power_costs "All power costs") all power costs modifier.
